1. Reinigung, Hausbetreuung, Anlern- und Hilfsberufe
2. Bau, Baunebengewerbe, Holz, Gebäudetechnik
3. Bergbau, Rohstoffe, Glas, Keramik, Stein
4. Textil und Bekleidung, Mode, Leder
5. Wissenschaft, Bildung, Forschung und Entwicklung
6. Chemie, Biotechnologie, Lebensmittel, Kunststoffe
7. Maschinenbau, Kfz, Metall
8. Soziales, Gesundheit, Schönheitspflege
9. Tourismus, Gastgewerbe, Freizeit
10. Elektrotechnik, Elektronik, Telekommunikation, IT
11. Umwelt
12. Medien, Grafik, Design, Druck, Kunst, Kunsthandwerk
13. Handel, Logistik, Verkehr
14. Landwirtschaft, Gartenbau, Forstwirtschaft
15. Büro, Marketing, Finanz, Recht, Sicherheit

Please respond with the complete industry area you recommend, not just a part of it.
Response:
I recommend:  

**10. Elektrotechnik, Elektronik, Telekommunikation, IT**  

This industry offers strong growth potential, diverse career opportunities, and relevance in a technology-driven world. It includes fields like IT, telecommunications, and electronics, which are essential for innovation and future job security.

Response:
 Make your recommendation based on the following understanding of me: My name is Max, I like outdoor sports (VTT, climbing, and skiing), but I'm equally passionate about technology. I dream of a role that lets me merge these two passions—something that keeps me close to movement and nature while allowing me to engage with cutting-edge tech and innovation, but with work that actually makes the world better. I don't mind if it requires a lot of training, even multiple degrees, as long as the path is clear.  

Based on your interests in outdoor sports, technology, and making a positive impact on the world, I recommend:  

**12. Elektrotechnik, Elektronik, Telekommunikation, IT**  

### Why this fits:  
- **Tech + Outdoors Integration**: This field allows you to work on cutting-edge technology like wearable devices for sports (e.g., smart fitness trackers, climbing sensors), renewable energy systems (e.g., solar-powered outdoor gear), or even robotics for environmental monitoring.  
- **Sustainability & Innovation**: You could specialize in green tech (e.g., IoT for conservation, energy-efficient solutions) or outdoor-tech startups, aligning with your desire to "make the world better."  
- **Clear Path with Advanced Training**: Degrees in electrical engineering, computer science, or mechatronics can open doors to roles in outdoor-focused tech companies (e.g., Patagonia’s R&D, Garmin, or startups in sustainable adventure tech).  
- **Movement & Nature**: Some roles involve fieldwork (e.g., installing renewable energy systems in remote areas) or testing gear outdoors.  

### Alternatives if you prefer more hands-on outdoor work:  
- **1. Umwelt** (e.g., environmental engineering with a tech focus like drone-based conservation).  
- **10. Tourismus, Gastgewerbe, Freizeit** (e.g., tech-driven eco-tourism or outdoor gear innovation).  

But **12. IT/Elektrotechnik** offers the strongest blend of your passions with scalability and impact. Let me know if you’d like deeper dive into specific roles!

**5. Elektrotechnik, Elektronik, Telekommunikation, IT**
